contest</h2><p class="StageHeader__body___6rSbL">Each week, we provide a cartoon in need of a caption. You, the reader, submit your caption below, we choose three finalists, and you vote for your favorite. Finalists for this week’s cartoon, by Farley Katz, will appear online September 10th and in the September 17, 2018, issue of The New Yorker. Anyone age thirteen or older can enter or vote.
